рдЗрддрд┐ [рдЪ] рдпреЛрдЬрдпрдиреНрддрд┐ ред

English

the further use of the word ekam
is, according to some, to disclose that

He who is the object of attainment
is Himself the means or up─Бya for that attainment

like the (celestial) kalpaka tree giving itself (to those that ask).

Thus (these commentators) suggest that
the use of “ekam” after “m─Бm” is to suggest the identity of the object of attainment
and the means of attaining it.

Espa├▒ol

el uso posterior de la palabra “ekam”
es, seg├║n algunos, revelar que

El que es el objeto de logro
es ├Йl mismo el medio o up─Бya para ese logro

como el ├бrbol (celestial) kalpaka entreg├бndose (a aquellos que piden).

Por lo tanto (estos comentaristas) sugieren que
el uso de “ekam” despu├йs de “m─Бm” es para sugerir la identidad del objeto de logro
y los medios para alcanzarlo.

English

This interpretation finds support in the sentence “m─Бm ekam eva” in a similar context :-

" By all means, seek the protection only of me alone
who am the inner self of all beings,
You will then have no fear of any kind."

Therefore he practises the up─Бya
revealed by the Lord,
with the help of the body and the senses given by Him

So it is improper for the intelligent aspirant to mukti
to consider himself, as another Siddhop─Бya equal to the Lord,
who is absolutely independent of others
and whose activities extend everywhere
and can meet with no hindrances or obstacles.
This is, according to these commentators, the purport of the word “eka” (only He and no other).

y cuyas actividades se extienden por todas partes
y puede cumplir sin obst├бculos.

If the statement that prapatti consists only in the acceptance of Siddhop─Бya were true,

(and not something to be done),

(and it would not lead to mokс╣гa ).

it would be opposed to the idea contained in the words of the Lord “┼Ыaraс╣Зam vraja” (seek me as the Saviour).

English

the Lord himself, who is endowed with the qualities essential for it,
stands as the Dispenser of the fruit desired,
without requiring any ancillary rite or dharma.
Therefore what is stated in the carama ┼Ыloka comes to this :-

“Bear this in mind
and seek Me alone for your salvation”.

Espa├▒ol

el Se├▒or mismo, que est├б dotado de las cualidades esenciales para ello,
se sit├║a como el Dispensador de la fruta deseada,
sin requerir ning├║n rito o dharma auxiliar.

Por lo tanto, lo que se dice en el carama ┼Ыloka viene a esto:-

“Ten esto en cuenta
y b├║scame s├│lo a M├н para tu salvaci├│n”.

But in prapatti, no other requisites are needed
except such as the will to do what is pleasing to the Lord -

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдПрд╖рд╛рдВ рдкреНрд░рд╕рд╛рджрди-рд╕реНрд╡рд░реВрдкреЗрдг

“рдорд╛рдореН рдПрдХрдореН” рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдЙрдЪреНрдпрддреЗ ред

English

The words, “m─Бm ekam” (me alone) are employed to show that,
in the case of the man destitute of other up─Бyas,

these ancillary dharmas other than prapatti are in no way connected with the Saviour
as the means of propitiating Him.

Espa├▒ol

Las palabras “m─Бm ekam” (yo solo) se emplean para mostrar que,
en el caso del hombre indigente de otros up─Бyas,

Estos dharmas auxiliares distintos de prapatti no est├бn de ninguna manera conectados con el Salvador
como medio para propiciarlo.

English

(6) This is also stated by some (commentators) -

as in the first half of the ┼Ыloka we find the words “sarva-dharm─Бn” (all dharmas)
and in the second half the word “sarva-p─Бpebhyo” (from all sins),
the word eka stands here as the counterpart or counterpoise to the word “all”.

Espa├▒ol

(6) Algunos (comentaristos) tambi├йn afirman de este modo-

como en la primera mitad del ┼Ыloka encontramos las palabras “sarva-dharm─Бn” (todos los dharmas)
y en la segunda mitad la palabra “sarva-p─Бpebhyo” (de todos los pecados),
la palabra “eka” est├б aqu├н como la contraparte o contrapeso de la palabra “todos”.

рджреБрд╖реНрдпрдиреНрдд рдЗрддрд┐ рдШреБрд╖реНрдпрддрд╛рдореН реереирейрее

English

If this be admitted, then the gist of the carama ┼Ыloka would be:

If a man is in despair
because of his inability to adopt such means or up─Бyas
as will yield the respective fruits desired by him,
then, I myself (single as I am) will stand for him as the respective means or up─Бya
to enable him to secure that fruit.

Espa├▒ol

Si se admite esto,
entonces la esencia del carama ┼Ыloka ser├нa:

Si un hombre est├б desesperado
debido a su incapacidad para adoptar tales medios o up─Бyas
como producir├б los respectivos frutos deseados por ├йl,

entonces, yo mismo (soltero como soy) representar├й a ├йl como el respectivo medio o up─Бya
para permitirle asegurar esa fruta.

рдЗрддреНрдердВ рдирд┐рдпрддрд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рддрдпрд╛ рднрдХреНрддрд┐-рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддреНрдпреЛрдГ рд╡рд┐рдХрд▓реНрдк-рд░реВрдкрд╛ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд┐рдГ,

English

That bhakti and prapatti stand as alternative up─Бyas
determined by the competence of the persons concerned
is evident from such passages as the following:

“I am capable of being attained
O, Thou of great wisdom,
either by deep bhakti or by prapatti
on the part of those who desire to render service to me,
I cannot be attained by any other means “.

Espa├▒ol

Que bhakti y prapatti son up─Бyas alternativos
determinado por la competencia de las personas interesadas
es evidente en pasajes como el siguiente:

“Yo soy capaz de ser alcanzado
Oh, t├║ de gran sabidur├нa,
ya sea por bhakti profundo o por prapatti
por parte de aquellos que desean prestarme servicio,
Yo no puedo ser alcanzado por ning├║n otro medio”.

(There is a well-known ┼Ыloka which says):-

“A man attains mokс╣гa
either by right knowledge,
or by death in the waters of the Gaс╣Еga
or by namask─Бra well-performed
or by bhakti “.

“Un hombre alcanza mokс╣гa

o por muerte en las aguas del Gaс╣Еga
o por namask─Бra bien interpretado

English

In such passages, those that are direct means of attaining mukti
are stated along with others that are not direct but only auxiliary.
This is only a way of exaggerating the importance of these indirect means.

Espa├▒ol

En tales pasajes, aquellos que son medios directos para alcanzar mukti
se indican junto con otras que no son directas sino s├│lo auxiliares.

English

There are some commentators who state that
the meaning of the word eka (a single one) declares that the Saviour is only one (namely, Bhagav─Бn)
and that ┼Ъr─л has nothing to do with salvation.
But their contention does not stand to reason.
Just as qualities and forms qualify the Lord as His attributes,
so also ┼Ъr─л is an attribute of His
(inseparable from Him).

Espa├▒ol

Hay algunos comentaristos que afirman que
el significado de la palabra eka (uno solo) declara que el Salvador es s├│lo uno (es decir, Bhagav─Бn)
y que ┼Ъr─л no tiene nada que ver con la salvaci├│n.

Pero su afirmaci├│n no es razonable.

As├н como las cualidades y formas califican al Se├▒or como Sus atributos,
as├н tambi├йn ┼Ъr─л es un atributo de Su
(inseparable de ├Йl).

and is dear to Bhagav─Бn
and is declared in the ┼Ыrutis as sharing in His duties
and as ever bent on protecting those that seek her help.

English

Though it is stated (in the Chandogya Upaniс╣гad and other Vedic texts)
that the material cause of the Universe is only one (sat),
yet other things that are requisite as material causes
are understood as existing as His attributes
(viz. cit and acit in their subtle and unmanifested forms)
on the authority of the pram─Бс╣Зas.
So also in this context, ┼Ъr─л should be understood,
although not distinctly stated.

Espa├▒ol

Aunque se afirma (en el Chandogya Upaniс╣гad y otros textos v├йdicos)
que la causa material del Universo es s├│lo una (sat),
otras cosas m├бs que son necesarias como causas materiales
se entienden como existentes como Sus atributos
(a saber, cit y acit en sus formas sutiles y no manifestadas)
sobre la autoridad de los pram─Бс╣Зas.
As├н tambi├йn en este contexto, ┼Ъr─л debe entenderse,
aunque no se indica claramente.

English

Even when a single form of up─Бsana or meditation is enjoined,
the qualities that are connected with the object of meditation enter also into it.
Similarly though a single deity is enjoined as the Saviour to be sought,
┼Ъr─л, who is His attribute,
should also be considered
as being associated with Him (in the act of salvation).

las cualidades que est├бn conectadas con el objeto de meditaci├│n entran tambi├йn en ├йl.
De manera similar, aunque se ordena una sola deidad como Salvador a ser buscado,
┼Ъr─л, quien es Su atributo,
Tambi├йn debe ser considerada
como estar asociada con ├Йl (en el acto de salvaci├│n).

English

Light and the object emitting light (are inseparable from each other)
and when one is mentioned ,
the other is also present by association. +++(5)+++

by virtue of their being always with each other.

Espa├▒ol

La luz y el objeto que la emite (son inseparables entre s├н)
y cuando uno se menciona,
el otro tambi├йn est├б presente por asociaci├│n. +++(5)+++
Del mismo modo, cuando cualquiera de (Bhagav─Бn o ┼Ъr─л) es mencionado, el otro tambi├йn est├б presente
en virtud de su estar siempre uno con el otro.

that she helps (j─лvas) to cross the sea of saс╣Бs─Бra
and both of them (Bhagav─Бn and ┼Ъr─л) have themselves spoken to the same effect in such (samhitas) treatises as s─Бtvatam.

Espa├▒ol

que ella ayuda (j─лvas) a cruzar el mar de saс╣Бs─Бra

English

In Dvaya it is considered appropriate that kaiс╣Еkarya or service in the state of attainment (mokс╣гa)
should extend to ┼Ъr─л (as to Bhagav─Бn).
So ┼Ъr─л is equally connected with Him in both the states,
that of the endeavour for attaining mokс╣гa (the first half of Dvaya)
and that after attainment (the second half of it).

Espa├▒ol

En Dvaya se considera apropiado que kaiс╣Еkarya o servicio en el estado de logro (mokс╣гa)
debe extenderse a ┼Ъr─л (como a Bhagav─Бn).
Entonces ┼Ъr─л est├б igualmente conectado con ├Йl en ambos estados,
el del esfuerzo por alcanzar mokс╣гa (la primera mitad de Dvaya)
y eso despu├йs de logro (la segunda mitad del mismo).
